route-policy TRANS_INT
  if (destination in MAS_24) then
    pass
  elseif (community matches-every 5) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 6) then
    set local-preference 98
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 7) then
    set local-preference 96
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 8) then
    set local-preference 94
    set community (8151:299, 8151:278) additive
  endif
end-policy

    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DUAL_HOMED
  if (community matches-every 1) then
    set local-preference 100
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 2) then
    set local-preference 98
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 3) then
    set local-preference 96
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 4) then
    set local-preference 94
    set community (no-export) additive
  elseif (community matches-every 5) then
    set local-preference 100
  elseif (community matches-every 6) then
    set local-preference 98
  elseif (community matches-every 7) then
    set local-preference 96
  elseif (community matches-every 8) then
    set local-preference 94
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MAO_CELAYA
  if (destination in MAO_CELAYA) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MAXAS_LIMIT
  if (as-path length ge 31) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy SAMECLUSTER
  if ((community matches-any SAMECLUSTER) and (destination in RUTA_CERO)) then
    pass
  elseif ((community matches-any TERCERRESPALDO) and (destination in RUTA_CERO)) then
    set local-preference 50
  elseif (destination in RUTA_CERO) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy MARCA_REGION
  set community (8151:648) additive
end-policy

  elseif (destination in RUTA_CERO) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy

end-policy
